Register

Register in LMSka

/register post

post

Register in LMSka

post /register

Register in LMSka

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • email: required(string)

    Email address

    Example:

    V@rte.im
  • password: required(string)

    Password

    Example:

    123456
  • telephone_number: required(string)

    Phone number

    Example:

    980009999
  • telephone_code: required(string)

    Phone number

    Example:

    38
  • first_name: required(string)

    First Name

    Example:

    John
  • last_name: required(string)

    Last Name

    Example:

    Doe
  • role_id: required(int)

    Role ID

    Example:

    5 (Student)

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Example:

result:

{
  "success": true,
  "message": "User was successfully registered but not verified"
}

/auth put

put

Login in LMSka

put /auth

post /forgotPassword

Restore password in LMSka

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • email: required(string)

    Account email

    Example:

    V@rte.im
  • is_staff: required(bool)

    default

    Example:

    false

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Example:

Update Profile

Update user profile data in LMSka

/updateProfile put

put

Update user profile data in LMSka

put /updateProfile

Update user profile data in LMSka

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • email: required(string)

    Email address

    Example:

    V@rte.im
  • telephone_number: required(string)

    Phone number

    Example:

    312312312
  • telephone_code: required(string)

    Phone number

    Example:

    380
  • first_name: required(string)

    First Name

    Example:

    John
  • last_name: required(string)

    Last Name

    Example:

    Doe

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Example:

result:

Update Avatar

Update user avatar in LMSka

/attachments post

post

Update user avatar in LMSka

post /attachments

Update user avatar in LMSka

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • file: required(string)

    File avatar

    Example:

    newAvatar.png
  • user: required(bool)

    Set true if user

    Example:

    true
  • user_logo: required(bool)

    Set true if avatar

    Example:

    true

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Example:

result:

{
  "path": "users/45/ava123.jpeg",
  "file_name": "ava123",
  "file_size": 10662,
  "extension": "jpeg",
  "attachment_type_id": 1,
  "user_id": 45,
  "updated_at": "2022-04-11T16:10:40.000000Z",
  "created_at": "2022-04-11T16:10:40.000000Z",
  "id": 138
}

  • Response
